This book isn’t like anything we have read by her and the art work/confession connection was completely <b>BRILLANT</b>! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492410739ra/22513854.gif' width='390' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The first half or more of this story is a total 5 PLUS Stars. The prologue was gripping while the way Owen and Auburn meet and his amazing art studio was perfection. The writing was just beautiful and</span>
  <span id="freeText11825282117012307966" style="display:none"><b>3.75 ~ 4 OMG Stars </b> <br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>I love Colleen Hoover's books for so many reasons but especially for the fact that each story isn't similar to the last book she has gifted her readers. This book isn’t like anything we have read by her and the art work/confession connection was completely <b>BRILLANT</b>! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492410739ra/22513854.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first half or more of this story is a total 5 PLUS Stars. The prologue was gripping while the way Owen and Auburn meet and his amazing art studio was perfection. The writing was just beautiful and similar to Maria from the Sound of Music spinning on the Alps I was in that much book happiness. <br><br><b>
  <i>"If I had known you would show up at my door one day. I'd have done everything differently. Everything."</i>
</b><br> <br>Sadly, somewhere amidst the crazy brother-in-law's antics, Auburn and Owen's lack of action in so many areas and their fast fall into love (I thought we would have had more scenes of them actually together) the story went a bit downhill for me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492410739ra/22513852.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fortunately in true Coho style the ending connects all areas of the plot and gifts a good sweet story in it's completion. <br><br><b>
  <i>"That could be fate, you know."</i>

<div id="review_988444111" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/988444111" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/988444111?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476791456" href="/book/show/22609310-confess">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer988444111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7665096710805378279"><a href='http://www.amazon.com/Confess-A-Novel-Colleen-Hoover-ebook/dp/B00LD1OHE0/ref=as_sl_pc_ss_til?tag=reaissex08-20&linkCode=w01&linkId=P34FVM2XICTOHFRG&creativeASIN=B00LD1OHE0' rel='nofollow noopener'>LIVE on AMAZON</a><br/><br/><a href='https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/confess/id894624198?mt=11&uo=4&at=1l3vwNR' rel='nofollow noopener'>LIVE on iTunes</a><br/><br/><i>Confess</i> is like nothing I have ever read before, it cannot be summed up in a few words. I have read a lot of books, but very few books have affected me the way this one did. I started this story late at night and within the first few pages I was crying and I knew this book would shake me to my core. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425818813i/13937736._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Auburn Reed has had an average life and you can definitely say things haven’t went according to plan. However, Auburn is one of the most resilient characters I have ever r</span>
  <span id="freeText7665096710805378279" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Confess-A-Novel-Colleen-Hoover-ebook/dp/B00LD1OHE0/ref=as_sl_pc_ss_til?tag=reaissex08-20&amp;linkCode=w01&amp;linkId=P34FVM2XICTOHFRG&amp;creativeASIN=B00LD1OHE0" rel="nofollow noopener">LIVE on AMAZON</a><br><br><a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/confess/id894624198?mt=11&amp;uo=4&amp;at=1l3vwNR" rel="nofollow noopener">LIVE on iTunes</a><br><br><i>Confess</i> is like nothing I have ever read before, it cannot be summed up in a few words. I have read a lot of books, but very few books have affected me the way this one did. I started this story late at night and within the first few pages I was crying and I knew this book would shake me to my core. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425818813i/13937736._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Auburn Reed has had an average life and you can definitely say things haven’t went according to plan. However, Auburn is one of the most resilient characters I have ever read and she isn’t going down without a fight. She is walking home one night in desperate need of a job when she stumbles across Owen Gentry, an artist looking for an assistant for his show. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I’m pretty sure you just made determination my favorite quality in a person.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Owen like most artist is eccentric and all over the place, but when he sees Auburn his life comes into focus. This isn’t a case of insta-love, it more about things lining up. He can see the life he wants to have, the life he deserves to have. However, he is also keeping a secret and it could destroy any chances he could ever have with Auburn. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425818813i/13937737._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I read this synopsis I immediately thought this would be your typical romance story. Coming from CoHo I knew it would be written well and engaging, but I cannot express how this story is so much more. I feel like <i>Confess</i> took writing to a whole other level. I know that is a big statement, but when I read this I was captivated on so many different levels. <br><br>At the beginning you read that all the confessions shared in the story are real anonymous confessions shared by readers. So while I read this story my heart broke for these anonymous people who shared a piece of themselves. Anonymous or not it is such a brave act to give a piece of yourself away, but more importantly to admit your feelings. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425818813i/13937738._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Someone recently asked me what <i>Confess</i> was about and I was at a loss, because this story isn’t about one thing to me. This story encompasses so many different things: love, loss, moving on, growing up, acceptance, forgiveness. <br><br>When I finished <i>Confess</i> I had no one to share it with, so I had my husband read the prologue. I wanted, no needed him to see why this book completely owned my thoughts. Today, weeks later it still owns my thoughts. I think about these characters as if they are real. I think about Auburn’s strength and determination. I think about Owen’s compassion and unconditional love. I think about the people who wrote confessions and are struggling with their own issues, and I am reminded we all have something. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425818813i/13937739._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I cannot recommend this book enough. It has so much heart and soul, and the story is beautifully delivered. <br><br>As a reader you know we get asked all the time: What’s your favorite book of all time? I have had the same favorite book of all time for years, until now, <i>Confess</i> is now my favorite book of all time. I sincerely hope everyone who reads this enjoys it even a little as much as I did. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. <br><br><br></i>
</b>

<div id="review_1100927018" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100927018" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1100927018?book_show_action=true">Nov 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476791456" href="/book/show/22609310-confess">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shower-smexin">shower-smexin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100927018" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12806077198720888855"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426080221i/13971247._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo confess love you forever_zps7xsudzpm.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><p>A new release from CoHo always attracts a HUGE amount of interest and deservedly so.  She’s a quality author with a large following, she’s very adept at social media (possibly the best), she’s funny and engaging and as such garners many auto 5 star reviews especially from the pre-release reviewers with ARCs which gush like crazy and extoll the book’s virtues and, having noticed this before, I raised a cynical eyebrow and vowed to read Confess with a highly critical eye and truly assess it on its</p></span>
  <span id="freeText12806077198720888855" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426080221i/13971247._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo confess love you forever_zps7xsudzpm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>A new release from CoHo always attracts a HUGE amount of interest and deservedly so.  She’s a quality author with a large following, she’s very adept at social media (possibly the best), she’s funny and engaging and as such garners many auto 5 star reviews especially from the pre-release reviewers with ARCs which gush like crazy and extoll the book’s virtues and, having noticed this before, I raised a cynical eyebrow and vowed to read Confess with a highly critical eye and truly assess it on its merits before reviewing.  In truth, I’m looking for fault.  So, as soon as the book downloaded to my Kindle I decided to adopt a total immersion technique, avoiding Goodreads and those stellar reviews like the plague, and plunged in head first without even reading the blurb to form my own opinions.</p><p>So, having decided to look for fault, I have to confess (get it????) that I actually found very little.  Possibly the story dragged a little at around the 60% mark and maybe the H and h didn’t get quite enough page time together as I would have liked but that was pretty much it and I think the conclusion to my experiment would be that she really does deserve all those rave reviews.  She’s right at the top of the new adult contemporary romance category, the undefeated champion of the genre and, even though there are plenty of pretenders for her crown, she ain’t going nowhere!</p><p>And so I began.  By 3% I was bawling my eyes out (rather like watching Pixar’s Up), by 15% I had the warm and fuzzies and was grinning like a loon into my Kindle, by 55% I was in the depths of despair and at 100% I sighed contentedly.  Job well done, CoHo.  I bought this on release day and had finished it by the evening –  it completely held my attention as I pretty much lost a whole day to this story.</p><p>In a Colleen Hoover novel there’s always a ‘thing’.  In Confess the 'thing' is art and our hero is Owen Mason Gentry (OMG) and he’s an artist whose work is inspired by confessions that are posted through his studio door.</p><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <strong>Every day I’m grateful that my husband and his brother look exactly alike. It means there’s less of a chance that my husband will find out that our son isn’t his.</strong>
  </p>
</blockquote><p>The confessions were brilliant – sometimes funny, sometimes sad, sometime shocking but it’s a truly original idea for a novel.</p><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <strong>I haven’t spoken to my children in four months. They’ll call on holidays and my birthday, but never in between. I don’t blame them. I was a horrible father.</strong>
  </p>
</blockquote><p>Auburn replies to his ‘Help Wanted’ sign on the door and this is how they meet although it’s obvious to us and Owen that he knows who she is but Auburn is oblivious to this.  I found myself instantly intrigued and dying to know what had happened in those intervening years between the prologue and now to bring us to the mysterious yet completely random meeting. By this point in the story, I was completely on board, totally hooked.  As the story continues, there’s such a stark contrast between the innocence of the young love of the prologue and the desperate situations both Auburn and Owen find themselves in, all due to the actions of others.  These two find themselves falling desperately in love and also realise that their being together would be the best yet worst thing that could happen to them.  They REALLY can’t be together – I am aware that that’s a highly common dilemma in new adult romance but the author works her magic here and puts a truly original spin on this and it’s completely believable and engrossing.</p><p>There’s a lot of secrets here, possibly truths as yet untold, and plenty of confessions will be required to get us towards the end of the story.  There appeared to be one glaring omission, one little fact not yet explained as we near the end of the book and I fretted, just a little, but I needn’t have worried – you can have faith in CoHo because she really does bring you full circle and everything is explained by the end of the book.  Hence the aforementioned contented sigh!</p><p>The pace of the story is gentle rather than slow which gives lots of time for the expansion of the growing affection of the two central characters and for us to become fully involved in this story which appears to hurtle from one disaster to the next although Colleen keeps everything grounded with strong character development and profound emotional depth. I felt every emotion with the characters, experiencing every high and low with them and was completely engrossed.  It’s a story that captured my interest from the very first page, kept me involved the whole way through and I found myself 100% emotionally invested.  The book had an almost magnetic pull on it - whenever I put it down, I soon found myself back, dying to continue.  Absolutely gripping stuff!</p><p>Reading a Colleen Hoover novel, to me, is rather like sinking into your favourite arm-chair after a hellish day at the office, kicking off those heels that have pinched all day and indulging in a glass of very expensive wine.  It’s exquisitely comforting and it feels like coming home.  I know I’m going to get a hero I will adore and a heroine I can identify with and that’s exactly what we found here. Heartbreakingly beautiful and achingly real, Confess is a wholly engrossing tale of two young people with many hurdles to overcome finding a love that is truly worth fighting for.  </p><p>
  <strong>4.5 OMG stars</strong>
</p><p>Owen’s paintings is based on a real artist – check out his beautiful work <a href="http://docart.bigcartel.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a></p></span>
  <a data-text-id="12806077198720888855" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

The first two chapters since I think you'd get the end more. Now the last chapter or the so-called 'twist' chapter, t</span>
  <span id="freeText6604755137973013555" style="display:none">I would truly love a chance to propose <b>an expirement</b> to my past before-i-read-this-book self. I'd tell her to do as followed:<br><br>Read the prologue which was from Auburn's pov and the first 2 chapters then go straight to the very last chapter 'five years earlier' told by Owen.<br><br>BAM!<br><br>A guaranteed 3 stars.<br><br>The prologue wasn't particularly good but just to orient myself with what's going on. The first two chapters since I think you'd get the end more. Now the last chapter or the so-called 'twist' chapter, that was good. Or maybe because I'd suffered through the whole book so that stood out in comparison? Could be.<br><br>Because the things in between were <b>either bland</b> (the romance), <b><i>really</i> bland</b> (the heroine) <b>or rather frustrating</b> (the evil mother-son duo coupled with our heroine's spinelessness).<br><br><br><a href="http://24.media.tumblr.com/ad5d70ca189ac12a3624c277bfaec00d/tumblr_ml9bnkuwiA1ryw2hqo1_500.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485060262ra/21781247.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>My very first Colleen Hoover book, after hearing about her from just about everyone on GR, I was <i>not</i> impressed.<br><br><br><b>rating: ★½</b><br><br><br><i>[edit] i revised this, many thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1902630-jokoloyo" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Jokoloyo</a> ❤<br><br></i></span>

<div id="review_1097134191" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1097134191" />
    <a title="Saania Zee Jamal ϟ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10376232-saania-zee-jamal"><img alt="Saania Zee Jamal ϟ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1495529362p2/10376232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1097134191?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saania Zee Jamal ϟ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saania Zee Jamal ϟ" href="/user/show/10376232-saania-zee-jamal">Saania Zee Jamal ϟ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476791456" href="/book/show/22609310-confess">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=fictional-non-fiction">fictional-non-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=quick-reads">quick-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=yawn">yawn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=covergasm">covergasm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=romance-shomance">romance-shomance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=cliched-fothermucker">cliched-fothermucker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=eh-ish">eh-ish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=massive-disappointment">massive-disappointment</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10376232-saania-zee-jamal?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1097134191" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13582080127174829714">One thing this book has convinced me of is Colleen Hoover's relentless ability to make even the most unrealistic of scenarios seem reasonable with her sway of writing; an ability I find both <u>admirable</u> and <u>annoying.</u><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“There are people you meet that you get to know, and then there are people you meet that you already know.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>There's a part towards the end of the book when the main characters themselves speculate how many times they've actually met each other, which boils down to a grand total of s</span>
  <span id="freeText13582080127174829714" style="display:none">One thing this book has convinced me of is Colleen Hoover's relentless ability to make even the most unrealistic of scenarios seem reasonable with her sway of writing; an ability I find both <u>admirable</u> and <u>annoying.</u><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“There are people you meet that you get to know, and then there are people you meet that you already know.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />There's a part towards the end of the book when the main characters themselves speculate how many times they've actually met each other, which boils down to a grand total of seven. <b>Seven</b> occasions (albeit not particularly interesting occasions either aside from tiny splashes of cute moments) it takes for them to fall madly in love with each other, but not even <b>one</b> to want to jump the other. I mean come <i>on</i>, she may do a fantastic job of weaving her words in such a way that the relationship really does seem to build up naturally– it worked on me with <i>Slammed</i>, but I'm afraid this time round, she simply couldn't work her magic.<br /><br />Because despite having at least some level of liking towards both Auburn and Owen, I didn't find myself falling much for their romance. It just- wasn't <i>palpable</i> enough, which for me, has to be the most important thing when reading a love story. And don't even get me started on the sheer number of times Owen said he deserved her<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[: the first time, I actually appreciated how this displayed a character that was confident about their self-worth and what they knew to be right, which isn't something you get to see too often in most contemporaries. Buuut then he had to go and repeat it 3928272 times in the middle of sex and make it stand out as WTF (I literally started considering whether or not this might cause a problem later on, but <i>nope</i>, it's enough to make our Auburn swoon some more. Eh, they deserve each other I guess) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. In fact, I'll even go as far as to say that <i>Adam</i> -bless his soul- was my favourite character of the book. <br /><br />I know I've only read about four Colleen Hoover novels so far, but I feel like she has this general formula: take two love interests, be sure to throw in some quirky traits there, add a dash of witty dialogue, mixed in with a whooole lot of <i>aggravating</i> misunderstandings, complications and tragedy, stirred by an underlying secret of sorts (one that isn't revealed until the very end so you have no choice but to want to keep reading), all topped off with a unique twist that sets the novel apart. <br /><br />Out of that, I have to say it's more or less the last ingredient that serves to keep me coming back for more– because like many of her other works, she is undeniably the undefeated queen of adding a special personal touch to every single book she writes. It is the reason Colleen Hoover is Colleen Hoover. The featured artwork alone (as well as the concept behind it, which btw, I WOULD LOVE TO SEE HAPPEN IN REAL LIFE IF IT HASN'T ALREADY) makes <i>Confess</i> deserve an extra star. But take away that and all you're left with is yet another mundane contemporary romance, with mundane main characters and an even more mundane deus ex machina.<br />___________________<br /><br /><b>Book song: Flames by P A T H</b><br />___________________</span>
  <a data-text-id="13582080127174829714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_987626355" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/987626355" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/987626355?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22667115-confess">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=all-time-fav-author">all-time-fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=in-the-minority">in-the-minority</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=imma-hit-that-bitch">imma-hit-that-bitch</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=standalones">standalones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=oh-look-pretty-cover">oh-look-pretty-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=dying-in-agony-of-wait">dying-in-agony-of-wait</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=release-march-2015">release-march-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer987626355" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11649304760868048910"><b>2.5 STARS ★★☆</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413400637ra/11505238.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>GAH. It absolutely pains me to once again give a CoHo book such a low rating :( Before anyone comes with a pitchfork at me, I just wanted to put it out there that I won't deny that CoHo writes beautifully and she's just one of those authors that I can expect to put out something different and unique with each read. This is no exception with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22609310.Confess' title='Confess by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Confess</a> as I found the concept to be very moving, for being able to read about actual confessions that had my heart squeezing and lastly to have</span>
  <span id="freeText11649304760868048910" style="display:none"><b>2.5 STARS ★★☆</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413400637ra/11505238.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>GAH. It absolutely pains me to once again give a CoHo book such a low rating :( Before anyone comes with a pitchfork at me, I just wanted to put it out there that I won't deny that CoHo writes beautifully and she's just one of those authors that I can expect to put out something different and unique with each read. This is no exception with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22609310.Confess" title="Confess by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Confess</a> as I found the concept to be very moving, for being able to read about actual confessions that had my heart squeezing and lastly to have it portrayed so vividly through real-life art was absolutely beautiful. <br><br>Sadly that was just the extent of how much I enjoyed the book because for the entire portion of the read, my emotions ranged from being baffled by these characters and mostly a whole lot of annoyance and frustration. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426095742ra/13973524.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'll start with the characters because to me, they came off completely two-dimensional. I struggled mostly trying to connect with them or at least understand the connection they're sharing. I felt that the entire read was a whole lot of "telling" but not enough "showing" to the extent that I failed to develop a sympathy for these characters for what they've been through. I wanted to <i>
  <b>feel</b>
</i> for them by myself but instead I felt like I was <i>
  <b>being told</b>
</i> how I should actually feel by their constant inner monologues. That really left me feeling very nonchalant during the entire read and it makes me sad that it didn't bring out the emotional depth I was looking for. <br><br>And there's Auburn who I really wanted to like and trust me, I've tried to let her grow on me but she just ended up coming off all wishy-washy. I'm not trying to come off insensitive given what she's been through and having never been in her shoes, naturally I found myself wanting to be more forgiving of her. But good lawd, I just got so frustrated by her lack of action to stand up for herself from time after time and right up to the point <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[where she nearly got raped by Trey and how she just wanted to let it slide <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, that's when I nearly lost my shit with this read. I went from baffled to almost appalled by the lack of backbone of this heroine and it really left a sour taste in my mouth as I read on :(<br><br>Another thing which left me really annoyed was also Trey's existence in the book that felt completely unnecessary and served purely as a plot device for the drama. Don't get me wrong, I'm an angst whore and I'm all in for jealousy play but Trey's involvement in this just came off as contrived drama and quite frankly, did not value to this read at all but instead it just made me want to skimmed through it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426147111ra/13980706.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The instalove portion of this book didn't peeved me as much but again, I was just left baffled by how quickly their relationship or feelings intensified after merely meeting each other for 24 hours. It was just all too rushed and Owen's strong inclination towards Auburn creeped me out a lot in the beginning. One thing I've always loved about CoHo's book are her boys that makes my heart pitter-patter and go all swoony over them but with Owen, there was a certain aloofness to him that never allowed me to warm up to his character.<br><br>As a huge fan of CoHo, I'm starting to feel really bummed that her current works have not been leaving me as much of an emotional impact like her previous. Perhaps it's just me or my expectations and I understand that it isn't fair for me to compare each of her work as they're always so different from the last and with her, there is no formulaic approach when it comes to her reads. <br><br>While I liked this one better than Ugly Love, it pains me to say that this one still turned out to be a lackluster for me :( As much as I still love her writing, I'm struggling to fall in love with her main characters anymore and the plot somehow seems to fade out as it progresses.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413223764ra/11480557.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With all that being said, I'm still very much looking forward to her next book because there's something about CoHo's writing that keeps me coming back for more. It's gripping and she constantly comes up with ideas that surprises her readers but sadly this one just wasn't for me again. <br><br><i><u>Confess</u> is a standalone NA contemporary romance novel.</i><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11649304760868048910" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1159606045" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1159606045" />
    <a title="Vilma Iris" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15777655-vilma-iris"><img alt="Vilma Iris" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1501855386p2/15777655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1159606045?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vilma Iris" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vilma Iris" href="/user/show/15777655-vilma-iris">Vilma Iris</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476791456" href="/book/show/22609310-confess">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1159606045" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7391393769802103220"><b>Compelling, fresh, heart wrenching and entirely unforgettable.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“I’m struggling for more air than I even need, but my panic is setting in, burying itself in my soul and making it hard to think. The sadness feels like warmth creeping its way up my chest, creating an insurmountable pressure the closer it gets to my heart.”</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>Bestselling author Colleen Hoover does it again. She delivers a compelling story with the power to evoke tears and laughs alike. Her trademark style emanates—both intense and e</span>
  <span id="freeText7391393769802103220" style="display:none"><b>Compelling, fresh, heart wrenching and entirely unforgettable.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“I’m struggling for more air than I even need, but my panic is setting in, burying itself in my soul and making it hard to think. The sadness feels like warmth creeping its way up my chest, creating an insurmountable pressure the closer it gets to my heart.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Bestselling author Colleen Hoover does it again. She delivers a compelling story with the power to evoke tears and laughs alike. Her trademark style emanates—both intense and effervescent, heartbreaking and heartswelling. Confess is a story that starts with a chance encounter and then twines in a way that seems destined and significant. Words hide secrets and confessions bleed off pages as Owen and Auburn find their way to each other, but not before loss furtively yields to new beginnings.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“I’ll love you forever. Even when I can’t.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Auburn’s life didn’t turn out quite as planned. By the time she was 20 years old, she had already been through more than most. But she needed to remain focused. So when by happenstance, she walks past a studio with a help wanted sign, she had to stop. She needed the money. But it was more than that, the windows beckoned her attention. They were covered in intimate and shocking confessions. The studio’s owner, Owen Gentry, is desperate for help, and when Auburn walks into the studio, Owen is immediately taken by this girl who is smart, sassy and somehow a little sad too.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“Are you here to save me?”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Both Auburn and Owen have secrets they bear, confessions they bury. As the story unfurls, the undercurrent of these unsaid words are felt, especially as Auburn’s heart-wrenching story comes to light, while Owen’s remains largely a mystery.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“Some secrets should never turn into confessions. I know that better than anyone.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />There are so many things I loved about this story. Colleen Hoover’s trademark mix of humor and heart. Real and striking confessions which came from readers. The art that brought the story to life in a beautifully abstract, yet emotionally acute way.<br /><br />So many things.<br /><br />Deception and pain, love and loss, secrets and truths, hope and redemption—they all twist and tangle together creating another unforgettable novel from one of the freshest and most trusted voices in romance. This book is not to be missed.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“I don’t feel lost in him at all, because it’s the first time I’ve ever felt like someone truly found me.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />✦ ✦ ✦ ✦<br /><br /><b> Follow Vilma's Book Blog: </b> <a href="http://vilmasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Website</a> | <a href="www.facebook.com/vilmasbookblog" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/vilmasbookblog" rel="nofollow noopener"> Twitter </a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7391393769802103220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_988547947" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/988547947" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/988547947?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476791456" href="/book/show/22609310-confess">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer988547947" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13835955923503524073"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br/>{BR with Dee, Mel and Sharon}<br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"I'll love you forever. Even when I can't."</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/adee8b1997385bb9e8f1178189b97d34_zpsthihjs9c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426376958i/14008279._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo adee8b1997385bb9e8f1178189b97d34_zpsthihjs9c.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>This is a story about a love that is lost and a love that is found. Auburn suffered a great loss when she was only 15 years old. Five years later, she finds herself living in a city, far from her family and dealing with problems that most 21 year old women would find impossible to handle.<br/><br/><br/><br/>Owen Mason Gentry, <b>OMG</b>, is a local artist whose paintings are based upon anonymous peoples' confessions that he</span>
  <span id="freeText13835955923503524073" style="display:none"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br>{BR with Dee, Mel and Sharon}<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I'll love you forever. Even when I can't."</b>
</i><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/adee8b1997385bb9e8f1178189b97d34_zpsthihjs9c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426376958i/14008279._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo adee8b1997385bb9e8f1178189b97d34_zpsthihjs9c.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This is a story about a love that is lost and a love that is found. Auburn suffered a great loss when she was only 15 years old. Five years later, she finds herself living in a city, far from her family and dealing with problems that most 21 year old women would find impossible to handle.<br><br><br><br>Owen Mason Gentry, <b>OMG</b>, is a local artist whose paintings are based upon anonymous peoples' confessions that he receives at his studio. He and Auburn meet one day when she is passing by his studio and starts reading the different confessions that are taped on his windows. He ends up offering her a job for the night, and there is an instant attraction between the two.<br><br><br><br>This is definitely not an "Insta-Love" story, and it will have you trying to figure out the secrets that both Owen and Auburn are keeping from each other. I did predict one of Owen's secrets but the rest came as a surprise to me.<br><br><br><br>I usually am over the moon in love with COHO's books, but I don't know why this one just didn't do it for me. I really liked Owen and I loved his humor. Don't get me started on the fact that he was an artist. I don't know what it is about an artist, but I find them utterly sexy!! The beginning dragged for me during some parts, and I actually skimmed a little. Once I got to the 60% mark and we get some revelations, I started to get into the story.<br><br><br><br>The ending was also anticlimactic. I mean, I did think what we find out in the end was pretty cool, <b>BUT</b>, I really wanted to see where both characters were in the future instead of going back to the past. Maybe it was the fact that I thought there was just too much going on that prevented me from falling in love with this story. It was an enjoyable read but in my opinion, not one of COHO's best.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer993664940307781006">I really liked this book! I only took one star from it because Owen had some weird issues with the word "deserve". I didn't dig the whole: You deserve me. I deserve you. It made me cringe. BUT everything else was perfect! The last chapter (the one that was 5 years ago) almost made me cry, I think I shed a little tear or two, it was beautiful. Also!   <span id="freeText993664940307781006" style="display:none">I really liked this book! I only took one star from it because Owen had some weird issues with the word "deserve". I didn't dig the whole: You deserve me. I deserve you. It made me cringe. BUT everything else was perfect! The last chapter (the one that was 5 years ago) almost made me cry, I think I shed a little tear or two, it was beautiful. Also! Auburn was a great female protagonist, I didn't really like Colleen's protagonist in her last two books (Tate in Ugly Love and Sydney in Maybe Someday, ugh, I want to punch them both), but Auburn I like, she's brave and funny and loving.<br /><br />I'm still waiting for Colleen to write a book that outstands her first books.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer988726030" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1733341622602654364"> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426077490i/13970980._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='294' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>What a beautiful story. I love how Colleen weaves different forms of art together, and the artwork in this book is stunning. I can always count on her to create phenomenal stories, and each experience is simply mesmerizing and unique. Within the first few pages, I had already shed a few tears, and I knew, <i>Confess</i> was going to be a great read. Auburn and Owen were perfection. They have both experienced so much heartbreak, they are selfless, relatable and simply loveable. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426077490i/13970981._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I'm not going to go i</span>
  <span id="freeText1733341622602654364" style="display:none"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426077490i/13970980._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="294" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>What a beautiful story. I love how Colleen weaves different forms of art together, and the artwork in this book is stunning. I can always count on her to create phenomenal stories, and each experience is simply mesmerizing and unique. Within the first few pages, I had already shed a few tears, and I knew, <i>Confess</i> was going to be a great read. Auburn and Owen were perfection. They have both experienced so much heartbreak, they are selfless, relatable and simply loveable. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426077490i/13970981._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'm not going to go into the plot. There is a bit of instalove, but I didn't care. The only reason this one isn't getting 5 stars from me is the second half, things went a little nuts, I lot was happening, maybe too much. My main issue was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trey. I could have done without him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I still really enjoyed this one and I would have loved more time with this couple. <br><br><i>
  <b> "That could be fate, you know." </b>
</i><br><br>**For anyone interested in the art from the book <br> <a href="http://docart.bigcartel.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Danny O'Connor</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1733341622602654364" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1435875383" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1435875383" />
    <a title="Riley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23179211-riley"><img alt="Riley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601446413p2/23179211.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1435875383?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Riley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Riley" href="/user/show/23179211-riley">Riley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476791456" href="/book/show/22609310-confess">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23179211-riley?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1435875383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17725832978665418946"><br/>I am very surprised by how much I disliked this, considering everything else I have read by Colleen Hoover I have given 5 stars. Confess is told in two points of views, Auburn, who lost the love of her life when she was only 15 and now at the age of 20 she desperately needs a job, which leads her to Owen, a young artist who is looking for an assistant. <br/><br/>The writing in this novel wasn’t the problem. In fact the writing was the only thing I liked. Colleen Hoover knows how to construct beautiful sen</span>
  <span id="freeText17725832978665418946" style="display:none"><br />I am very surprised by how much I disliked this, considering everything else I have read by Colleen Hoover I have given 5 stars. Confess is told in two points of views, Auburn, who lost the love of her life when she was only 15 and now at the age of 20 she desperately needs a job, which leads her to Owen, a young artist who is looking for an assistant. <br /><br />The writing in this novel wasn’t the problem. In fact the writing was the only thing I liked. Colleen Hoover knows how to construct beautiful sentences and because of that I was blinded for the first half of the book into believing I loved it. Once I was able to see past the beautiful writing I was able to see all the problems. <br /><br />The characters in the book were awful. Auburn was so passive I couldn’t take it. She had no backbone and refused to stand up for herself. It seemed like she was just waiting for someone to swoop in and save her rather than fight to fix her own problems which irritated me so much. <br /><br />For as much as I disliked Auburn, Owen was worse. Firstly, he went on and on about how all of his previous relationships failed because he couldn’t stand his ex-girlfriends. But then he says that he’s always the one that gets dumped so I think we know what the real problem is here. <br /><br />It annoyed me so much how he constantly told Auburn he is the only person in the world that deserved her. He told her that so much I wanted to puke. In the scene where they finally have sex he says the word “deserve” 7 times. Like dude. It’s not romantic, it’s just creepy. <br /><br />We learn early on in the book that Owen knows Auburn and about her past, but she doesn’t know him. And we don’t find out how he knows her until the last few pages of the book. But what really frustrated me was that he kept this big secret from her the entire book and it’s never resolved! And I really feel like not wrapping that up was just a cop out.<br /><br />The romance in the book really didn’t work for me. I felt like we were told they were in love but I never saw it. It was like I blinked and missed it happening. I don’t know what they saw in each other. They really didn’t have any chemistry. <br /><br />Other than the writing I did really love the artwork that was in this book. It was beautiful and added a lot more to the story. Something I love about Colleen Hoovers books is that she always takes that extra step to add something special to her books. While I didn’t like this book I do still love her writing but this book just fell short for me. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17725832978665418946" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18297204468365443541"><b>
  <i>“I’ll love you forever. Even when I can’t”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426334072i/14003145.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay, this is hands-down the best Colleen Hoover book I have ever read, and I can’t stop crying!<br/><br/>I loved the characters in this book. Auburn was so sweet, and tried so hard even when the odds were stacked against her, and Owen went above and beyond the call of duty to help his father, even when his father didn’t thank him for it.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"It's just such a long walk from work to home, and long walks make me contemplate my life, and my life makes me cry."</i>

  <i>“I’ll love you forever. Even when I can’t”</i>

Auburn was so sweet, and tried so hard even when the odds were stacked against her, and Owen went above and beyond the call of duty to help his father, even when his father didn’t thank him for it.<br><br><b>
  <i>"It's just such a long walk from work to home, and long walks make me contemplate my life, and my life makes me cry."</i>

This book surprised me more than once, and it was such a pleasure to read! I have to say that I am not usually a big Colleen Hoover fan, I normally give her books 3 stars, but this one was just beautiful. I loved the struggles, I loved how the pieces all slowly came together, and I loved the romance.<br><br><b>
  <i>"It's been a long time since I've wanted someone to kiss me.<br>Or maybe it's just been a long time since I've allowed myself to feel this way."</i>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/987527485" />
    <a title="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog"><img alt="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596881564p2/6603203.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/987527485?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  " href="/user/show/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog">Pavlina Read more sleep less blog❤❤  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476791456" href="/book/show/22609310-confess">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog?shelf=best-cover">best-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6603203-pavlina-read-more-sleep-less-blog?shelf=want-to-read-soon">want-to-read-soon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer987527485" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3538910794095990647"> <b> 4 STARS<br/><br/>"That could be fate, you know." </b><br/><br/>I'ts long time since I have read a book from Colleen Hoover as I haven't read Ugly Love so I can say that I really missed her writing! This author is so charismatic. Each of her books have so many emotions and her stories are unique. I find this story so brilliant, the confessions from different people which become paintings and the fact that there were pictures of the paintings inside the book make it even more captivating!The prologue and the ending was</span>
  <span id="freeText3538910794095990647" style="display:none"> <b> 4 STARS<br><br>"That could be fate, you know." </b><br><br>I'ts long time since I have read a book from Colleen Hoover as I haven't read Ugly Love so I can say that I really missed her writing! This author is so charismatic. Each of her books have so many emotions and her stories are unique. I find this story so brilliant, the confessions from different people which become paintings and the fact that there were pictures of the paintings inside the book make it even more captivating!The prologue and the ending was intense and I cried while I was reading.<br><br>The story:Auburn is living in Texas and she needs a second job. While she was walking she sees an art studio. Owen is the owner and the artist who creates his paintings from Confessions which people leave in his studio.We see the attraction between them but Auburn knows that it isn't the time for a relationship because there is someone else who cares for him a lot...I will not say what exactly he is to her because if I say it's a spoiler... I don't want to give anything else.I feel that if I say more it will reveal the story so you need to read it to learn! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426248529i/13992405._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both characters are a little mysterious as both have some secrets that they don't reveal from the beginning.I loved that they give a little of themselves at perfect times.I'm not sure if I should say their love was insta or not exactly but we see the bond from the beginning and the relationship between Owen and Auburn moved fast .I liked Owen because he is sweet and I loved his passion for the art! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426118852i/13976984._SX540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>What I wanted more?I wanted to see more of Auburn and Owen as a couple.What I didn't like?I didn't like Trey and Lydia at all.Especially Lydia for the way she treated Auburn and Trey for everything!I think he is really sick! The only thing I didn't like about Auburn is that she didn't say anything to them..I know her reasons but she could have done something sooner!<br> <br>I can't say it's my favorite book but still the writing and the brilliant story make it a wonderful story! I really think I should buy it in paperback because of all these images of paintings inside the book!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('04123jtclfAXOZLnwgFFCI/JtJF9PkkLAHUtGJXQvB8oebb2mGm3Cej23WBVjM2XuH//7baYmCXwHvaS1Z88Kw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GoLkmQRYpSWdoL1G3nLDSPNH9Oc97eVPQABGDVZiKxjhdiSxp22H3GJv8sFJ/0vXxPG/m/ZLNGGwa52HFi2rLA==')})
  }
